***дискутировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дискутировать.html>дискути́ровать</a> (27054)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">diskutieren</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">discutere</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дискутировать.html>дискути́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">diskutírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to discuss, to debate <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">participate in a discussion or debate</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>дис<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ку<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ти.html>ти́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ро<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вать</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 2a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-дискут-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-ир-ова</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:диспозиция.html>диспози́ция</a> (24810)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">dispositiō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">arrangement</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:диспозиция.html>диспози́ция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dispozícija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:диспозиция.html>диспози́ции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:диспозиция.html>диспози́ции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:диспозиция.html>диспози́ций</a></b>)

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:диссонанс.html>диссона́нс</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dissonáns</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:диссонанс.html>диссона́нса</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:диссонанс.html>диссона́нсы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:диссонанс.html>диссона́нсов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music<span class="ib-comma">,</span> linguistics<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dissonance</li></ol>

Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>дис-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-сон-</b>; суффикс: <b>-анс</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<ol><li>remote-controlled

<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дистанционный.html>дистанцио́нное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обучение.html>обуче́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">distanciónnoje obučénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">distance learning</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дисциплинарный.html>дисциплина́рный</a> (26697)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">disciplinary</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***дитя.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дитя.html>дитя́</a> (5922)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">дѣтя</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dětja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dětę</i>. The <i><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a></i> of the first syllable in the singular is from <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">дити́на</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ditína</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, nowadays written <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:детина.html>дети́на</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">detína</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> by analogy with the accented <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>де́ти</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">déti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with regular distant assimilation <i>ѣ</i>…<i><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и́</a></i> gt; <i><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a></i>…<i><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и́</a></i>. An alternative formulation by Šakhmatov (<i>ѣ</i> gt; <i><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a></i> before a soft consonant) explains these forms more directly.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дитя.html>дитя́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ditjá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дитя.html>дитя́ти</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>де́ти</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>дете́й</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">see note on oblique forms</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated or poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> child, baby, kid (also used ironically or in similes)</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>The oblique cases of singular <i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дитя.html>дитя́</a></b></i>, except for the accusative case, are never used in speech and seldom in modern prose writing, as many native speakers do not intuitively understand their exact inflectional roles in relation to <i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дитя.html>дитя́</a></b></i>, and may consider them strange or even Un-Russian. Instead, the corresponding cases of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребёнок</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rebjónok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> are used.</li>
<li>The plural forms are standard and in common use, and serve as the normal plural forms of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребёнок</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rebjónok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребёнок</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rebjónok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:детка.html>де́тка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">détka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:детеныш.html>детёныш</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">detjónyš</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">детёнок</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">detjónok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">rare</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:детский.html>де́тский</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">détskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:детвора.html>детвора́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">detvorá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дитя.html>дитя́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ditjá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ди.html>ди</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>тя́</b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:длань.html>дла́нь</a> (26441)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu"><a href = vnd.unilang:длань.html>дла́нь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dlanĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ладонь.html>ладо́нь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ladónʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the inherited Old East Slavic form.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:длинный.html>дли́нный</a> (416)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:длина.html>длина́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dliná</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:длинный.html>дли́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dlínnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)длинне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)длинне́й</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">длинне́йший</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>long, lengthy</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> ironic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tall, lanky <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a person</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can we date this quote?)</span>,  Mikhail Bulgakov,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Master_and_Margarita" class="extiw" title="w:Master and Margarita">The Master and Margarita</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>Но</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:увы.html>увы́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:длинный.html>дли́нный</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:сквозь.html>сквозь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рого</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:видно.html>ви́дно</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:гражданин.html>граждани́н</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:касаться.html>каса́ясь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:земля.html>земли</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качаться.html>кача́лся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ним</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:влево.html>вле́во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вправо.html>впра́во</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">No éto, uvý, býlo, i <b>dlínnyj</b>, skvozʹ kotórovo vídno, graždanín, ne kasájasʹ zemli, kačálsja pered nim i vlévo i vprávo.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">But, unfortunately, it was happening [for real], and a <b>lanky</b>, see-through citizen was swaying in front of him left and right without touching the ground.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">short form only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> too long, longer than necessary <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of clothing and shoes</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́ти</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:штаны.html>штаны́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:длинный.html>длинны́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mne éti štaný <b>dlinný</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">these trousers are too long for me</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:длина.html>дли́н</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a/c". <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i>длинне́е, длинне́й, подлинне́е, подлинне́й.</i>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-длин-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порядочный.html>-н</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-дл-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-ин-н</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b>  | Кузнецова, Ефремова, 1986 | .

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">denʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ник</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дневник.html>дневни́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dnevník</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дневник.html>дневника́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дневник.html>дневники́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дневник.html>дневнико́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>diary</li>
<li>journal, datebook, daybook</li>
<li>school record book</li></ol>
